\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Some\ important\ concepts\ to\ understand\ to\ use\ this\ library:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Codepoint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Characters\ are\ defined\ by\ unicode\ codepoints,\ e.g.\ 65\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ uppercase\ A,\ 231\ is\ lowercase\ c\ with\ a\ cedilla,\ 0x7e30\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ hiragana\ for\ "{}ma"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Glyph}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ some\ glyph)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Glyph\ index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ font-\/specific\ integer\ ID\ representing\ a\ glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Baseline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Glyph\ shapes\ are\ defined\ relative\ to\ a\ baseline,\ which\ is\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ bottom\ of\ uppercase\ characters.\ Characters\ extend\ both\ above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ below\ the\ baseline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Current\ Point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ As\ you\ draw\ text\ to\ the\ screen,\ you\ keep\ track\ of\ a\ "{}current\ point"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ which\ is\ the\ origin\ of\ each\ character.\ The\ current\ point's\ vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ position\ is\ the\ baseline.\ Even\ "{}baked\ fonts"{}\ use\ this\ model.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Vertical\ Font\ Metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ vertical\ qualities\ of\ the\ font,\ used\ to\ vertically\ position}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ space\ the\ characters.\ See\ docs\ for\ stbtt\_GetFontVMetrics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ Font\ Size\ in\ Pixels\ or\ Points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ preferred\ interface\ for\ specifying\ font\ sizes\ in\ stb\_truetype}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ is\ to\ specify\ how\ tall\ the\ font's\ vertical\ extent\ should\ be\ in\ pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ that\ sounds\ good\ enough,\ skip\ the\ next\ paragraph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Most\ font\ APIs\ instead\ use\ "{}points"{},\ which\ are\ a\ common\ typographic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ measurement\ for\ describing\ font\ size,\ defined\ as\ 72\ points\ per\ inch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stb\_truetype\ provides\ a\ point\ API\ for\ compatibility.\ However,\ true}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}per\ inch"{}\ conventions\ don't\ make\ much\ sense\ on\ computer\ displays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ since\ different\ monitors\ have\ different\ number\ of\ pixels\ per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ inch.\ For\ example,\ Windows\ traditionally\ uses\ a\ convention\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ there\ are\ 96\ pixels\ per\ inch,\ thus\ making\ 'inch'\ measurements\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00187\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ nothing\ to\ do\ with\ inches,\ and\ thus\ effectively\ defining\ a\ point\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ be\ 1.333\ pixels.\ Additionally,\ the\ TrueType\ font\ data\ provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00189\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ an\ explicit\ scale\ factor\ to\ scale\ a\ given\ font's\ glyphs\ to\ points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00190\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ but\ the\ author\ has\ observed\ that\ this\ scale\ factor\ is\ often\ wrong}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00191\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ non-\/commercial\ fonts,\ thus\ making\ fonts\ scaled\ in\ points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00192\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ according\ to\ the\ TrueType\ spec\ incoherently\ sized\ in\ practice.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00197\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Select\ how\ high\ you\ want\ the\ font\ to\ be,\ in\ points\ or\ pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00198\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Call\ ScaleForPixelHeight\ or\ ScaleForMappingEmToPixels\ to\ compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00199\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ a\ scale\ factor\ SF\ that\ will\ be\ used\ by\ all\ other\ functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ Baseline:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ You\ need\ to\ select\ a\ y-\/coordinate\ that\ is\ the\ baseline\ of\ where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ your\ text\ will\ appear.\ Call\ GetFontBoundingBox\ to\ get\ the\ baseline-\/relative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ bounding\ box\ for\ all\ characters.\ SF*-\/y0\ will\ be\ the\ distance\ in\ pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ that\ the\ worst-\/case\ character\ could\ extend\ above\ the\ baseline,\ so\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ you\ want\ the\ top\ edge\ of\ characters\ to\ appear\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ screen\ where\ y=0,\ then\ you\ would\ set\ the\ baseline\ to\ SF*-\/y0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ Current\ point:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Set\ the\ current\ point\ where\ the\ first\ character\ will\ appear.\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ first\ character\ could\ extend\ left\ of\ the\ current\ point;\ this\ is\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ dependent.\ You\ can\ either\ choose\ a\ current\ point\ that\ is\ the\ leftmost}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ point\ and\ hope,\ or\ add\ some\ padding,\ or\ check\ the\ bounding\ box\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ left-\/side-\/bearing\ of\ the\ first\ character\ to\ be\ displayed\ and\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ the\ current\ point\ based\ on\ that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00216\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00217\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ Displaying\ a\ character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00218\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Compute\ the\ bounding\ box\ of\ the\ character.\ It\ will\ contain\ signed\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00219\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ relative\ to\ <current\_point,\ baseline>.\ I.e.\ if\ it\ returns\ x0,y0,x1,y1,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00220\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ then\ the\ character\ should\ be\ displayed\ in\ the\ rectangle\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00221\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ <current\_point+SF*x0,\ baseline+SF*y0>\ to\ <current\_point+SF*x1,baseline+SF*y1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00222\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00223\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ Advancing\ for\ the\ next\ character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00224\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Call\ GlyphHMetrics,\ and\ compute\ 'current\_point\ +=\ SF\ *\ advance'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00225\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00226\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00227\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ADVANCED\ USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00228\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00229\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Quality:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00230\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00231\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Use\ the\ functions\ with\ Subpixel\ at\ the\ end\ to\ allow\ your\ characters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00232\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ to\ have\ subpixel\ positioning.\ Since\ the\ font\ is\ anti-\/aliased,\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00233\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ hinted,\ this\ is\ very\ import\ for\ quality.\ (This\ is\ not\ possible\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00234\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ baked\ fonts.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00235\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00236\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Kerning\ is\ now\ supported,\ and\ if\ you're\ supporting\ subpixel\ rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00237\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ then\ kerning\ is\ worth\ using\ to\ give\ your\ text\ a\ polished\ look.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00238\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00239\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Performance:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00240\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00241\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Convert\ Unicode\ codepoints\ to\ glyph\ indexes\ and\ operate\ on\ the\ glyphs;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00242\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ if\ you\ don't\ do\ this,\ stb\_truetype\ is\ forced\ to\ do\ the\ conversion\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00243\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ every\ call.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00244\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00245\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ There\ are\ a\ lot\ of\ memory\ allocations.\ We\ should\ modify\ it\ to\ take}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00246\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ a\ temp\ buffer\ and\ allocate\ from\ the\ temp\ buffer\ (without\ freeing),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00247\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ should\ help\ performance\ a\ lot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00248\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00249\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ NOTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00250\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00251\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ The\ system\ uses\ the\ raw\ data\ found\ in\ the\ .ttf\ file\ without\ changing\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00252\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ and\ without\ building\ auxiliary\ data\ structures.\ This\ is\ a\ bit\ inefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00253\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ on\ little-\/endian\ systems\ (the\ data\ is\ big-\/endian),\ but\ assuming\ you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00254\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ caching\ the\ bitmaps\ or\ glyph\ shapes\ this\ shouldn't\ be\ a\ big\ deal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00255\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00256\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ It\ appears\ to\ be\ very\ hard\ to\ programmatically\ determine\ what\ font\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00257\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ given\ file\ is\ in\ a\ general\ way.\ I\ provide\ an\ API\ for\ this,\ but\ I\ don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00258\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ recommend\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00259\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ PERFORMANCE\ MEASUREMENTS\ FOR\ 1.06:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00950\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ These\ functions\ compute\ a\ discretized\ SDF\ field\ for\ a\ single\ character,\ suitable\ for\ storing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00951\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ a\ single-\/channel\ texture,\ sampling\ with\ bilinear\ filtering,\ and\ testing\ against}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00952\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ larger\ than\ some\ threshold\ to\ produce\ scalable\ fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00953\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ info\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ the\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00954\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scale\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ controls\ the\ size\ of\ the\ resulting\ SDF\ bitmap,\ same\ as\ it\ would\ be\ creating\ a\ regular\ bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00955\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ glyph/codepoint\ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ the\ character\ to\ generate\ the\ SDF\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00956\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ padding\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ extra\ "{}pixels"{}\ around\ the\ character\ which\ are\ filled\ with\ the\ distance\ to\ the\ character\ (not\ 0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00957\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ which\ allows\ effects\ like\ bit\ outlines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00958\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ onedge\_value\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ value\ 0-\/255\ to\ test\ the\ SDF\ against\ to\ reconstruct\ the\ character\ (i.e.\ the\ isocontour\ of\ the\ character)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00959\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pixel\_dist\_scale\ \ -\/-\/\ \ what\ value\ the\ SDF\ should\ increase\ by\ when\ moving\ one\ SDF\ "{}pixel"{}\ away\ from\ the\ edge\ (on\ the\ 0..255\ scale)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00960\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ positive,\ >\ onedge\_value\ is\ inside;\ if\ negative,\ <\ onedge\_value\ is\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00961\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ width,height\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ output\ height\ \&\ width\ of\ the\ SDF\ bitmap\ (including\ padding)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00962\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xoff,yoff\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ output\ origin\ of\ the\ character}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00963\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ value\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ \ a\ 2D\ array\ of\ bytes\ 0..255,\ width*height\ in\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00964\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00965\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ pixel\_dist\_scale\ \&\ onedge\_value\ are\ a\ scale\ \&\ bias\ that\ allows\ you\ to\ make}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00966\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ optimal\ use\ of\ the\ limited\ 0..255\ for\ your\ application,\ trading\ off\ precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00967\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ special\ effects.\ SDF\ values\ outside\ the\ range\ 0..255\ are\ clamped\ to\ 0..255.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00968\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00969\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00970\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ scale\ =\ stbtt\_ScaleForPixelHeight(22)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00971\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ padding\ =\ 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00972\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ onedge\_value\ =\ 180}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00973\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ pixel\_dist\_scale\ =\ 180/5.0\ =\ 36.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00974\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00975\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ This\ will\ create\ an\ SDF\ bitmap\ in\ which\ the\ character\ is\ about\ 22\ pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00976\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ high\ but\ the\ whole\ bitmap\ is\ about\ 22+5+5=32\ pixels\ high.\ To\ produce\ a\ filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00977\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ shape,\ sample\ the\ SDF\ at\ each\ pixel\ and\ fill\ the\ pixel\ if\ the\ SDF\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00978\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ is\ greater\ than\ or\ equal\ to\ 180/255.\ (You'll\ actually\ want\ to\ antialias,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00979\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ which\ is\ beyond\ the\ scope\ of\ this\ example.)\ Additionally,\ you\ can\ compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00980\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ offset\ outlines\ (e.g.\ to\ stroke\ the\ character\ border\ inside\ \&\ outside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00981\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ or\ only\ outside).\ For\ example,\ to\ fill\ outside\ the\ character\ up\ to\ 3\ SDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00982\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ pixels,\ you\ would\ compare\ against\ (180-\/36.0*3)/255\ =\ 72/255.\ The\ above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00983\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ choice\ of\ variables\ maps\ a\ range\ from\ 5\ pixels\ outside\ the\ shape\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00984\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ 2\ pixels\ inside\ the\ shape\ to\ 0..255;\ this\ is\ intended\ primarily\ for\ apply}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00985\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ outside\ effects\ only\ (the\ interior\ range\ is\ needed\ to\ allow\ proper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00986\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ antialiasing\ of\ the\ font\ at\ *smaller*\ sizes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00987\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00988\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ function\ computes\ the\ SDF\ analytically\ at\ each\ SDF\ pixel,\ not\ by\ e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00989\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ building\ a\ higher-\/res\ bitmap\ and\ approximating\ it.\ In\ theory\ the\ quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00990\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ should\ be\ as\ high\ as\ possible\ for\ an\ SDF\ of\ this\ size\ \&\ representation,\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00991\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ unclear\ if\ this\ is\ true\ in\ practice\ (perhaps\ building\ a\ higher-\/res\ bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00992\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ computing\ from\ that\ can\ allow\ drop-\/out\ prevention).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00993\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00994\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ algorithm\ has\ not\ been\ optimized\ at\ all,\ so\ expect\ it\ to\ be\ slow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00995\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ if\ computing\ lots\ of\ characters\ or\ very\ large\ sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00996\ }
